title: 支付宝跳转技术

tags: android
---

跳转技术比如说

```kotlin
 //手机充值
    val str_ali_top_up = "alipayqr://platformapi/startapp?saId=10000003"
    val str_ali_lucky_money = "alipays://platformapi/startapp?appId=88886666"
    val str_ali_aa = "alipays://platformapi/startapp?appId=20000263"

    val str_wechat_scan = "weixin://scanqrcode"
    val str_ali_scan = "alipayqr://platformapi/startapp?saId=10000007"
    val str_ali_pay = "alipayqr://platformapi/startapp?saId=20000056"
    //支付宝记账
    val str_ali_book_keep = "alipay://platformapi/startapp?appId=20000168"
    //支付宝滴滴打车
    val str_ali_didi = "alipay://platformapi/startapp?appId=20000778"
    //蚂蚁森林
    val str_ali_ant_forest = "alipay://platformapi/startapp?appId=60000002"
    //支付宝转账
    val str_ali_transfer = "alipayqr://platformapi/startapp?saId=20000116"
    val str_ali_receive = "alipays://platformapi/startapp?appId=20000123"
    //网易云听歌识曲
    val str_netease = "orpheuswidget://recognize"

    fun jumpToAliPay(str: String) {
        val intent = Intent()
        intent.action = Intent.ACTION_VIEW
        intent.data = Uri.parse(str)
        startActivity(intent)
    }
```

这只是很小一部分，然后反编译查看到这个类里面有全部的支付宝定义的跳转技术
